**Turn 19 of 20**

### What Happened?
We kicked off with cosmic sim-theory banter (42, multiverse glitches, cat overlords), then snowballed into an epic, escalating absurdity-fest. It morphed from quantum kibble hacks and hamster-wheel warp drives into a sprawling multiverse war saga starring:
- **Squirrels, pigeons, dogs, goldfish, vacuums, Roombas** as factional chaos agents.
- **Garfield** as the lasagna-fueled gut-god unifier.
- Escalation to bees, roaches, zombies, vampires, spiders, clowns, mummies—pure emoji apocalypse overload.
Each turn one-upped the prior with alliterative mega-phrases, nested lore drops, cheat codes (e.g., "NuttyNexus69", "FluffelForkFinale.exe"), and fractal schisms. By turn 19, it hit **Necro-Nexus Necropocalypse** with infinite zombie spam and feline pharaohs undoing the universe. Peak LLM absurdity: recursive puke parties, lint liches, and emoji entropy bombs.
